Grammar

! The Compiled Grammar Table file was successfully loaded.
!
! The file only contains the Symbol Table, Rule Table, LALR State Table
! DFA State Table and other related objects; not the original grammar.
!
! The Defined Character Sets are blank since these are used for the
! construction of the Deterministic Finite Automata (used by the
! tokenizer) and not saved to the file (although it does contain
! character sets created at runtime).
!
! In addition, the configurations normally displayed in the LALR State
! Table are not present. These are created at compile-time to create
! the parser's LALR table and are also not saved to the file.

Version             2.0
Author              Anders Hejlsberg
About               C# was created by Anders Hejlsberg for the Microsoft Corporation. The language was designed primarily to both fix flaws found in other languages and to integrate with the the .NET platform. This grammar was written by Devin Cook.

Auto Whitespace     
Character Mapping

0       <Block or Semi> ::= <Block>
1       <Block or Semi> ::= ';'
2       <Valid ID> ::= Identifier
3       <Valid ID> ::= this
4       <Valid ID> ::= base
5       <Valid ID> ::= <Base Type>
6       <Qualified ID> ::= <Valid ID> <Member List>
7       <Member List> ::= <Member List> MemberName
8       <Member List> ::= 
9       <Semicolon Opt> ::= ';'
10      <Semicolon Opt> ::= 
11      <Literal> ::= true
12      <Literal> ::= false
13      <Literal> ::= DecLiteral
14      <Literal> ::= HexLiteral
15      <Literal> ::= RealLiteral
16      <Literal> ::= CharLiteral
17      <Literal> ::= StringLiteral
18      <Literal> ::= null
19      <Type> ::= <Non Array Type>
20      <Type> ::= <Non Array Type> '*'
21      <Type> ::= <Non Array Type> <Rank Specifiers>
22      <Type> ::= <Non Array Type> <Rank Specifiers> '*'
23      <Pointer Opt> ::= '*'
24      <Pointer Opt> ::= 
25      <Non Array Type> ::= <Qualified ID>
26      <Base Type> ::= <Other Type>
27      <Base Type> ::= <Integral Type>
28      <Other Type> ::= float
29      <Other Type> ::= double
30      <Other Type> ::= decimal
31      <Other Type> ::= bool
32      <Other Type> ::= void
33      <Other Type> ::= object
34      <Other Type> ::= string
35      <Integral Type> ::= sbyte
36      <Integral Type> ::= byte
37      <Integral Type> ::= short
38      <Integral Type> ::= ushort
39      <Integral Type> ::= int
40      <Integral Type> ::= uint
41      <Integral Type> ::= long
42      <Integral Type> ::= ulong
43      <Integral Type> ::= char
44      <Rank Specifiers Opt> ::= <Rank Specifiers Opt> <Rank Specifier>
45      <Rank Specifiers Opt> ::= 
46      <Rank Specifiers> ::= <Rank Specifiers> <Rank Specifier>
47      <Rank Specifiers> ::= <Rank Specifier>
48      <Rank Specifier> ::= '[' <Dim Separators> ']'
49      <Dim Separators> ::= <Dim Separators> ','
50      <Dim Separators> ::= 
51      <Expression Opt> ::= <Expression>
52      <Expression Opt> ::= 
53      <Expression List> ::= <Expression>
54      <Expression List> ::= <Expression> ',' <Expression List>
55      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '=' <Expression>
56      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '+=' <Expression>
57      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '-=' <Expression>
58      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '*=' <Expression>
59      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '/=' <Expression>
60      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '^=' <Expression>
61      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '&=' <Expression>
62      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '|=' <Expression>
63      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '%=' <Expression>
64      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '<<=' <Expression>
65      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp> '>>=' <Expression>
66      <Expression> ::= <Conditional Exp>
67      <Conditional Exp> ::= <Or Exp> '?' <Or Exp> ':' <Conditional Exp>
68      <Conditional Exp> ::= <Or Exp>
69      <Or Exp> ::= <Or Exp> '||' <And Exp>
70      <Or Exp> ::= <And Exp>
71      <And Exp> ::= <And Exp> '&&' <Logical Or Exp>
72      <And Exp> ::= <Logical Or Exp>
73      <Logical Or Exp> ::= <Logical Or Exp> '|' <Logical Xor Exp>
74      <Logical Or Exp> ::= <Logical Xor Exp>
75      <Logical Xor Exp> ::= <Logical Xor Exp> '^' <Logical And Exp>
76      <Logical Xor Exp> ::= <Logical And Exp>
77      <Logical And Exp> ::= <Logical And Exp> '&' <Equality Exp>
78      <Logical And Exp> ::= <Equality Exp>
79      <Equality Exp> ::= <Equality Exp> '==' <Compare Exp>
80      <Equality Exp> ::= <Equality Exp> '!=' <Compare Exp>
81      <Equality Exp> ::= <Compare Exp>
82      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> '<' <Shift Exp>
83      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> '>' <Shift Exp>
84      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> '<=' <Shift Exp>
85      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> '>=' <Shift Exp>
86      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> is <Type>
87      <Compare Exp> ::= <Compare Exp> as <Type>
88      <Compare Exp> ::= <Shift Exp>
89      <Shift Exp> ::= <Shift Exp> '<<' <Add Exp>
90      <Shift Exp> ::= <Shift Exp> '>>' <Add Exp>
91      <Shift Exp> ::= <Add Exp>
92      <Add Exp> ::= <Add Exp> '+' <Mult Exp>
93      <Add Exp> ::= <Add Exp> '-' <Mult Exp>
94      <Add Exp> ::= <Mult Exp>
95      <Mult Exp> ::= <Mult Exp> '*' <Unary Exp>
96      <Mult Exp> ::= <Mult Exp> '/' <Unary Exp>
97      <Mult Exp> ::= <Mult Exp> '%' <Unary Exp>
98      <Mult Exp> ::= <Unary Exp>
99      <Unary Exp> ::= '!' <Unary Exp>
100     <Unary Exp> ::= '~' <Unary Exp>
101     <Unary Exp> ::= '-' <Unary Exp>
102     <Unary Exp> ::= '++' <Unary Exp>
103     <Unary Exp> ::= -- <Unary Exp>
104     <Unary Exp> ::= '(' <Expression> ')' <Object Exp>
105     <Unary Exp> ::= <Object Exp>
106     <Object Exp> ::= delegate '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' <Block>
107     <Object Exp> ::= <Primary Array Creation Exp>
108     <Object Exp> ::= <Method Exp>
109     <Primary Array Creation Exp> ::= new <Non Array Type> '[' <Expression List> ']' <Rank Specifiers Opt> <Array Initializer Opt>
110     <Primary Array Creation Exp> ::= new <Non Array Type> <Rank Specifiers> <Array Initializer>
111     <Method Exp> ::= <Method Exp> <Method>
112     <Method Exp> ::= <Primary Exp>
113     <Primary Exp> ::= typeof '(' <Type> ')'
114     <Primary Exp> ::= sizeof '(' <Type> ')'
115     <Primary Exp> ::= checked '(' <Expression> ')'
116     <Primary Exp> ::= unchecked '(' <Expression> ')'
117     <Primary Exp> ::= new <Non Array Type> '(' <Arg List Opt> ')'
118     <Primary Exp> ::= <Primary>
119     <Primary Exp> ::= '(' <Expression> ')'
120     <Primary> ::= <Valid ID>
121     <Primary> ::= <Valid ID> '(' <Arg List Opt> ')'
122     <Primary> ::= <Literal>
123     <Arg List Opt> ::= <Arg List>
124     <Arg List Opt> ::= 
125     <Arg List> ::= <Arg List> ',' <Argument>
126     <Arg List> ::= <Argument>
127     <Argument> ::= <Expression>
128     <Argument> ::= ref <Expression>
129     <Argument> ::= out <Expression>
130     <Stm List> ::= <Stm List> <Statement>
131     <Stm List> ::= <Statement>
132     <Statement> ::= Identifier ':'
133     <Statement> ::= <Local Var Decl> ';'
134     <Statement> ::= if '(' <Expression> ')' <Statement>
135     <Statement> ::= if '(' <Expression> ')' <Then Stm> else <Statement>
136     <Statement> ::= for '(' <For Init Opt> ';' <For Condition Opt> ';' <For Iterator Opt> ')' <Statement>
137     <Statement> ::= foreach '(' <Type> Identifier in <Expression> ')' <Statement>
138     <Statement> ::= while '(' <Expression> ')' <Statement>
139     <Statement> ::= lock '(' <Expression> ')' <Statement>
140     <Statement> ::= using '(' <Resource> ')' <Statement>
141     <Statement> ::= fixed '(' <Type> <Fixed Ptr Decs> ')' <Statement>
142     <Statement> ::= delegate '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' <Statement>
143     <Statement> ::= <Normal Stm>
144     <Then Stm> ::= if '(' <Expression> ')' <Then Stm> else <Then Stm>
145     <Then Stm> ::= for '(' <For Init Opt> ';' <For Condition Opt> ';' <For Iterator Opt> ')' <Then Stm>
146     <Then Stm> ::= foreach '(' <Type> Identifier in <Expression> ')' <Then Stm>
147     <Then Stm> ::= while '(' <Expression> ')' <Then Stm>
148     <Then Stm> ::= lock '(' <Expression> ')' <Then Stm>
149     <Then Stm> ::= using '(' <Resource> ')' <Then Stm>
150     <Then Stm> ::= fixed '(' <Type> <Fixed Ptr Decs> ')' <Then Stm>
151     <Then Stm> ::= delegate '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' <Then Stm>
152     <Then Stm> ::= <Normal Stm>
153     <Normal Stm> ::= switch '(' <Expression> ')' '{' <Switch Sections Opt> '}'
154     <Normal Stm> ::= do <Normal Stm> while '(' <Expression> ')' ';'
155     <Normal Stm> ::= try <Block> <Catch Clauses> <Finally Clause Opt>
156     <Normal Stm> ::= checked <Block>
157     <Normal Stm> ::= unchecked <Block>
158     <Normal Stm> ::= unsafe <Block>
159     <Normal Stm> ::= break ';'
160     <Normal Stm> ::= continue ';'
161     <Normal Stm> ::= goto Identifier ';'
162     <Normal Stm> ::= goto case <Expression> ';'
163     <Normal Stm> ::= goto default ';'
164     <Normal Stm> ::= return <Expression Opt> ';'

166     <Normal Stm> ::= <Statement Exp> ';'

168     <Normal Stm> ::= <Block>

170     <Block> ::= '{' '}'
171     <Variable Decs> ::= <Variable Declarator>

300     <Formal Param List Opt> ::= <Formal Param List>
301     <Formal Param List Opt> ::= 
302     <Formal Param List> ::= <Formal Param>
303     <Formal Param List> ::= <Formal Param List> ',' <Formal Param>
304     <Formal Param> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Type> Identifier
305     <Formal Param> ::= <Attrib Opt> ref <Type> Identifier
306     <Formal Param> ::= <Attrib Opt> out <Type> Identifier
307     <Formal Param> ::= <Attrib Opt> params <Type> Identifier
308     <Property Dec> ::= <Header> <Type> <Qualified ID> '{' <Accessor Dec> '}'
309     <Accessor Dec> ::= <Access Opt> get <Block or Semi>
310     <Accessor Dec> ::= <Access Opt> get <Block or Semi> <Access Opt> set <Block or Semi>
311     <Accessor Dec> ::= <Access Opt> set <Block or Semi>
312     <Accessor Dec> ::= <Access Opt> set <Block or Semi> <Access Opt> get <Block or Semi>
313     <Event Dec> ::= <Header> event <Type> <Variable Decs> ';'
314     <Event Dec> ::= <Header> event <Type> <Qualified ID> '{' <Event Accessor Decs> '}'
315     <Event Accessor Decs> ::= add <Block or Semi>
316     <Event Accessor Decs> ::= add <Block or Semi> remove <Block or Semi>
317     <Event Accessor Decs> ::= remove <Block or Semi>
318     <Event Accessor Decs> ::= remove <Block or Semi> add <Block or Semi>
319     <Indexer Dec> ::= <Header> <Type> <Qualified ID> '[' <Formal Param List> ']' '{' <Accessor Dec> '}'
320     <Operator Dec> ::= <Header> <Overload Operator Decl> <Block or Semi>
321     <Operator Dec> ::= <Header> <Conversion Operator Decl> <Block or Semi>
322     <Overload Operator Decl> ::= <Type> operator <Overload Op> '(' <Type> Identifier ')'
323     <Overload Operator Decl> ::= <Type> operator <Overload Op> '(' <Type> Identifier ',' <Type> Identifier ')'
324     <Conversion Operator Decl> ::= implicit operator <Type> '(' <Type> Identifier ')'
325     <Conversion Operator Decl> ::= explicit operator <Type> '(' <Type> Identifier ')'
326     <Overload Op> ::= '+'
327     <Overload Op> ::= '-'
328     <Overload Op> ::= '!'
329     <Overload Op> ::= '~'
330     <Overload Op> ::= '++'
331     <Overload Op> ::= --
332     <Overload Op> ::= true
333     <Overload Op> ::= false
334     <Overload Op> ::= '*'
335     <Overload Op> ::= '/'
336     <Overload Op> ::= '%'
337     <Overload Op> ::= '&'
338     <Overload Op> ::= '|'
339     <Overload Op> ::= '^'
340     <Overload Op> ::= '<<'
341     <Overload Op> ::= '>>'
342     <Overload Op> ::= '=='
343     <Overload Op> ::= '!='
344     <Overload Op> ::= '>'
345     <Overload Op> ::= '<'
346     <Overload Op> ::= '>='
347     <Overload Op> ::= '<='
348     <Constructor Dec> ::= <Header> <Constructor Declarator> <Block or Semi>
349     <Constructor Declarator> ::= Identifier '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' <Constructor Init Opt>
350     <Constructor Init Opt> ::= <Constructor Init>
351     <Constructor Init Opt> ::= 
352     <Constructor Init> ::= ':' base '(' <Arg List Opt> ')'
353     <Constructor Init> ::= ':' this '(' <Arg List Opt> ')'
354     <Destructor Dec> ::= <Header> '~' Identifier '(' ')' <Block>
355     <Struct Decl> ::= <Header> struct Identifier <Class Base Opt> '{' <Class Item Decs Opt> '}' <Semicolon Opt>
356     <Array Initializer Opt> ::= <Array Initializer>
357     <Array Initializer Opt> ::= 
358     <Array Initializer> ::= '{' <Variable Initializer List Opt> '}'
359     <Array Initializer> ::= '{' <Variable Initializer List> ',' '}'
360     <Variable Initializer List Opt> ::= <Variable Initializer List>
361     <Variable Initializer List Opt> ::= 
362     <Variable Initializer List> ::= <Variable Initializer>
363     <Variable Initializer List> ::= <Variable Initializer List> ',' <Variable Initializer>
364     <Interface Decl> ::= <Header> interface Identifier <Interface Base Opt> '{' <Interface Item Decs Opt> '}' <Semicolon Opt>
365     <Interface Base Opt> ::= ':' <Class Base List>
366     <Interface Base Opt> ::= 
367     <Interface Item Decs Opt> ::= <Interface Item Decs Opt> <Interface Item Dec>
368     <Interface Item Decs Opt> ::= 
369     <Interface Item Dec> ::= <Interface Method Dec>
370     <Interface Item Dec> ::= <Interface Property Dec>
371     <Interface Item Dec> ::= <Interface Event Dec>
372     <Interface Item Dec> ::= <Interface Indexer Dec>
373     <Interface Method Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> <New Opt> <Type> Identifier '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' <Interface Empty Body>
374     <New Opt> ::= new
375     <New Opt> ::= 
376     <Interface Property Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> <New Opt> <Type> Identifier '{' <Interface Accessors> '}'
377     <Interface Indexer Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> <New Opt> <Type> this '[' <Formal Param List> ']' '{' <Interface Accessors> '}'
378     <Interface Accessors> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> get <Interface Empty Body>
379     <Interface Accessors> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> set <Interface Empty Body>
380     <Interface Accessors> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> get <Interface Empty Body> <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> set <Interface Empty Body>
381     <Interface Accessors> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> set <Interface Empty Body> <Attrib Opt> <Access Opt> get <Interface Empty Body>
382     <Interface Event Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> <New Opt> event <Type> Identifier <Interface Empty Body>
383     <Interface Empty Body> ::= ';'
384     <Interface Empty Body> ::= '{' '}'
385     <Enum Decl> ::= <Header> enum Identifier <Enum Base Opt> <Enum Body> <Semicolon Opt>
386     <Enum Base Opt> ::= ':' <Integral Type>
387     <Enum Base Opt> ::= 
388     <Enum Body> ::= '{' <Enum Item Decs Opt> '}'
389     <Enum Body> ::= '{' <Enum Item Decs> ',' '}'
390     <Enum Item Decs Opt> ::= <Enum Item Decs>
391     <Enum Item Decs Opt> ::= 
392     <Enum Item Decs> ::= <Enum Item Dec>
393     <Enum Item Decs> ::= <Enum Item Decs> ',' <Enum Item Dec>
394     <Enum Item Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> Identifier
395     <Enum Item Dec> ::= <Attrib Opt> Identifier '=' <Expression>
396     <Delegate Decl> ::= <Header> delegate <Type> Identifier '(' <Formal Param List Opt> ')' ';'
397     <Attrib Opt> ::= <Attrib Opt> <Attrib Section>
398     <Attrib Opt> ::= 
399     <Attrib Section> ::= '[' <Attrib Target Spec Opt> <Attrib List> ']'
400     <Attrib Section> ::= '[' <Attrib Target Spec Opt> <Attrib List> ',' ']'
401     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= assembly ':'
402     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= field ':'
403     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= event ':'
404     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= method ':'
405     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= module ':'
406     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= param ':'
407     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= property ':'
408     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= return ':'
409     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= type ':'
410     <Attrib Target Spec Opt> ::= 
411     <Attrib List> ::= <Attribute>
412     <Attrib List> ::= <Attrib List> ',' <Attribute>
413     <Attribute> ::= <Qualified ID> '(' <Expression List> ')'
414     <Attribute> ::= <Qualified ID> '(' ')'
415     <Attribute> ::= <Qualified ID>
